       <h1 class="page-header">Procurement Services</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab5"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff-directories/index.html">Staff &amp; directories</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="supplier-information/index.html">Supplier information</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="policies-forms/index.html">Policies &amp; forms</a></li>

     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We develop and implement systemwide purchasing policies and strategies.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>Procurement Services aims to provide efficient and effective purchasing services in support of the university's mission, sourcing the highest quality of products and services at the least total cost. We leverage university buying power through strategic and collaborative sourcing, adoption of proven technologies&nbsp;and supplier performance management. Procurement Services also works to create a culture that expects continuous improvement in cost, quality and service.&nbsp;<a href="about-procurement-services.html">Read more</a></p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="William Cooper" src="_images/bill-cooper.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> William Cooper </p> 
         <p>Associate Vice President &amp; Chief Procurement Officer</p> 
        </div> 
       </div>

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <img src="/Images/employees.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Ensure Your FERPA Compliance</h3> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9"> 
      <span class="warning">Important:</span> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
       <li>For definitions of what constitutes &quot;personally identifiable information&quot; or &quot;educational records,&quot; see <a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/_files/ed-affairs/ferpa101.pdf" target="_blank">UC FERPA 101</a>.</li> 
       <li><a href="/registrar/help-desk/default.aspx">Our office</a> handles all official transcripts and subpoena requests.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Your Access</h3> 
      <p>You have access to a student's educational records for the sole purpose of performing your job responsibly. You are granted this access as a school official with &quot;legitimate educational interest.&quot; This is defined as:</p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>Performing a task specified in a position description or contract</li> 
       <li>Performing a task related to a students education or discipline</li> 
       <li>Providing a service to a student</li> 
       <li>Maintaining safety and security on campus</li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-9 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <img src="/Images/folder.png" style="float: right; margin: 4px;" /> 
       <div class="title">
         FERPA Resources: 
       </div> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="http://www.ucop.edu/general-counsel/_files/ed-affairs/ferpa101.pdf" target="_new">UC FERPA 101</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.ed.gov/policy/gen/guid/fpco/ferpa/index.html" target="_new">US Department of Education and FERPA</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://policy.ucop.edu/doc/2710533/PACAOS-130" target="_new">UC FERPA Policy</a></li> 
        <li><a href="../privacy-ferpa/ucr-ferpa-policy.aspx">UCR FERPA Policy</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www.dol.gov/dol/ppii.htm" target="_new">US Protection of Personal Information Policies</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://www2.ed.gov/policy/gen/guid/fpco/index.html" target="_new">US Department of Education Family Policy Compliance Office</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <h3>Your Responsibilities</h3> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets wide"> 
       <li>You have a responsibility to protect the confidentiality of a students educational records, regardless of the medium in which those records are presented.</li> 
       <li>Posting grades using the student's name, student ID number or any portion of the social security number violates FERPA.</li> 
       <li>You may not disclose personally identifiable information about a student nor permit inspection of a students educational records without that students written consent (e.g., a signed department-specific release form).</li> 
       <li>It is your responsibility to verify that student directory information is not restricted before releasing it. You can view which information a student has restricted on screen 011 in the Student Information System.</li> 
       <li>Reference letters written on behalf of a student do not give you authorization to disclose that students records or performance details without that students written consent (e.g., a signed department-specific release form.</li> 
       <li>In general, student information may only be shared with the students consent, in a health or safety emergency, or pursuant to another FERPA exception.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Required FERPA Training (Subject to Change)</h3> 
      <p>UCR employees (and student employees) who want to access the Student Information System (SIS) must complete special training and sign a statement of FERPA understanding. <a href="http://emsystems.ucr.edu/Pages/SISTraining.aspx" target="_blank">You can do both online here.</a></p> 
      <h3>How Can Students Release Records?</h3> 
      <p>Students can customize their public directory information, authorize Growl users (e.g., family) and sign department-specific release forms. See <a href="/registrar/privacy-ferpa/disclosure-policies.aspx">Disclosure Policies</a> for more details.</p> 
      <h3>About Department-Specific Release Forms</h3> 
      <p>Your department may modify this <a href="/content/pdfs/permission_to_release_educational_records.pdf" target="_blank">Permission to Release Educational Records</a> form. Its a way for students to grant your department permission to release their records to third parties. It must be completed prior to the disclosure of any private information. </p> 
      <h3>Questions?</h3> 
      <p>FERPA questions should be directed to the Campus FERPA Officer at 951-827-3427 or via email (<a href="mailto:bracken.dailey@ucr.edu">bracken.dailey@ucr.edu</a>). </p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div>

     <h3>UCR Budget and Financial Snapshot</h3> 
     <div class="xpander"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="ucrsnapshotcontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
      <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
      <ul> 
       <li><a title="UCR Budget Overview and Funding Sources" href="/documents/budget/UCR_Budget_Overview_and_Funding_Sources.pdf" target="_blank">UCR Budget Overview and Funding Sources</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a title="UCR Spending" href="/documents/budget/UCR_Spending.pdf" target="_blank">UCR Spending</a></li>

     <h3>UCR Budget Information</h3> 
     <div class="xpander"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="ucrbudgetcontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
      <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/staffing/2013-14_Staffing_and_Permanent_Budget_Instructions_Letter_to_Campus.pdf" target="_blank">2013-14 Staffing and Permanent Budget Letter to Campus</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Permanent Budget Reports</h4> 
      <p>The Permanent Budget is the reoccurring annual allocation of funds and/or fiscal plan that renews each year as of July 1.</p> 
      <h5>Function Summary</h5> 
      <p>These reports provide July 1 Permanent Budget data by functional area.&nbsp; Function classifies budgetary and expenditure transactions by general program categories such as; instruction, research, and institutional support, etc.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/function_summary.pdf" target="_blank">Current Year</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/function_summary_3-year.pdf" target="_blank">Three-year summary</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget/function_definitions.pdf" target="_blank">Function Definitions</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5>Budget Category Summary</h5> 
      <p>These reports provide July 1 Permanent Budget data by budget category. Budget Category represents the budget level for a grouping of expense accounts.&nbsp; For example, the budget category Supplies &amp; Expense includes funding for supplies, travel, communication, depreciation expense, etc.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/budget_category_summary.pdf" target="_blank">Current Year</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/Income%20Resources%20Summary-Three%20Year%20Summary%202013.pdf" target="_blank">Three-year summary</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5>Income Resources summary</h5> 
      <p>These reports provide July 1 Permanent Budget data by fund group. Income sources represent broad categories (fund groups) of revenues available to fund Campus Operations.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/Income%20Resources%20Summary-Current%20Year%202013.pdf" target="_blank">Current Year</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/Income%20Resources%20Summary-Three%20Year%20Summary%202013.pdf" target="_blank">Three-year summary</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5>Organizational Summary</h5> 
      <p>These reports provide July 1 Permanent Budget data by Campus Organization.</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/Organizational%20Summary-Current%20Year%202013-1.pdf" target="_blank">Current Year</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/organizational_summary_5-year.pdf" target="_blank">Five-year summary</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h6>Prior Year Summaries</h6> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/perm_budget_org_summary_2007.pdf" target="_blank">July 1, 2007</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/perm_budget_org_summary_2008.pdf" target="_blank">July 1, 2008</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/perm_budget_org_summary_2009.pdf" target="_blank">July 1, 2009</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/budget_summary_org_and_fund_group_2011.pdf" target="_blank">July 1, 2010</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/budget_summary/budget_2012_org_group_summary.pdf" target="_blank">July 1, 2011</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <p><a href="http://budget.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Campus Budget News</a></p>
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
     </div> 
     <h3>UCR Staffing Information</h3> 
     <div class="xpander"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="ucrstaffcontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
      <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/staffing/Staffing_Instructions_FY_2013.pdf" target="_blank">Staffing Instructions FY2013</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/staffing/2013-14_Staffing_and_Permanent_Budget_Instructions_Letter_to_Campus.pdf" target="_blank">2013-14 Staffing and Permanent Budget Letter to Campus</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>Staffing Reports</h4> 
      <p>These reports provide July 1 Permanent Budget data and FTE (Full Time Equivalent), data from the Payroll &amp; Personnel System (PPS), and the Open Provision file from UCRFS (UCR Financial System).</p> 
      <h5>Five-Year History Faculty FTE Summary</h5> This report contains summary data I&amp;R, OR, and the Health Sciences Faculty FTE by Organization as of the census dates of October 31 for each fiscal year 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/Five-Year%20History-10-31-13.pdf" target="_blank">Five-Year History </a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5>Current Year Faculty FTE Census Data</h5> This report contains I&amp;R, OR, and Health Sciences Faculty FTE summary data by Department. 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/documents/irhealthsciencescensus.pdf" target="_blank">Instruction &amp; Research and Health Sciences Faculty FTE</a></li> 
       <li><a href="/documents/Organized%20Research%20Faculty%20FTE%20-%2010-31-13.pdf" target="_blank">Organized Research Faculty FTE</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h5><a href="/documents/staffing/academic-staff_fte_summary_by_organization.pdf" target="_blank">Academic /Staff FTE Summary by Organization</a></h5> 
      <h5><a href="/documents/staffing/staff_fte_by_functional_summary.pdf" target="_blank">Staff FTE by Functional Summary</a></h5>
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
     </div> 
     <h3>UCR Financial Information</h3> 
     <div class="xpander"> 
      <h3>Organizational Information Sheets</h3> 
      <div class="xpander"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="orginfocontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
       <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
       <p>The Organizational Informational Sheets are a management tool that gives a snapshot view of each Organization over a three-year period. The reported information is concise and common across a majority of the Organizations and contains data such as expenditures, carry-forward balances, FTE, and statistical data.</p> 
       <p>The Organizational Information Sheets are developed after all annual reporting is complete for the applicable fiscal year and are generally available in February.</p> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="/2012-13%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf">2012-13 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2011-12%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2011-12 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2010-11%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2010-11 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2009-10_organization_information_sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2009-10 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2008-09%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2008-09 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2007-08%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2007-08 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2006-07%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2006-07 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/reports/2005-06%20Organization%20Information%20Sheets.pdf" target="_blank">2005-06 Organization Information Sheets</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/documents/budget/list_of_classifications-org_info_sheets.pdf" target="_blank">List of Classifications - Org Info Sheets</a></li> 
       </ul>
       <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      </div> 
      <h3>Overview of Fund Uses</h3> 
      <div class="xpander"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="overviewfundcontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
       <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="/documents/fund_group_classification.pdf" target="_blank">Fund Group Classifications</a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <p>What is the make-up of funding at UCR compared to the entire UC system?</p> 
       <h5>Current Fund Receipts by Fund Group</h5> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a title="FY11-12 Revenue Pie Chart - UCR and UC" href="/documents/FY11-12%20Revenue%20Pie%20Chart%20-%20UCR%20and%20UC.pdf" target="_blank">FY11-12 Revenue Pie Chart - UCR and UC.pdf</a></li>

        <li><a href="/documents/budget/fy07-08_revenue_pie_chart_r-ucr_and_uc.pdf" target="_blank">FY07-08 Revenue Pie Chart (Revised) - UCR and UC.pdf</a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <h5>Current Fund Expenditures by Fund Group</h5> 
       <ul>

      <h3>Annual Contract and Grant Expenditure Reports</h3> 
      <div class="xpander"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="annualcontent" group="Everyone" button="707" -->
       <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="700"/ -->
       <p>These reports provide data on actual expenditures, direct and facilities and administration (F&amp;A), associated with contracts and grants awarded to the University of California, Riverside (UCR) by non-University entities.&nbsp; Data is provided at the Organization and Departmental level as reflected in the Campuss General Ledger.</p>

<p>&nbsp;The Support Rate Analysis
provides a broad framework of measures to assess the financial flexibility of
funding in support of the fundamental teaching and research mission of the
University.</p>
<p>The figures in this report represent faculty support from
various fund sources grouped into several categories.&nbsp; Category 1 represents the permanent General Fund/Core
budget available for academic support, while Categories 2, 3, and 4 reflect
actual expenditures.&nbsp; Certain
departmental units, accounts, and funds which do not represent faculty
support were excluded from the analysis.&nbsp;
In all but Category 4 general fund (19900, 19903, 19904 and 19906)
employee benefits were excluded.</p>
